<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">autheur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">autor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">auctor</i>.
</p>

***autochtoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:autochtoon.html>autochtoon</a> (77300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">αὐτόχθων</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">autókhthōn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">indigenous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:autochtoon.html>autochtoon</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:autochtoon.html>autochtoner</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">autochtoonst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>autochthonous</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:autochtoon.html>autochtoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:autochtonen.html>autochtonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:autochtoon.html>autochtoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***automaat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:automaat.html>automaat</a> (14070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">αὐτόματον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">autómaton</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Subsequently influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">automate</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:automaat.html>automaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:automaten.html>automaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:automaat.html>automaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a machine that performs automated tasks</li>
<li>an automatic, a car with an automatic transmission</li>
<li>an automaton</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">automatenhal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">drankautomaat</span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkoopautomaat.html>verkoopautomaat</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:automatiek.html>automatiek</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***automatisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:automatisch.html>automatisch</a> (5964)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:automatisch.html>automatisch</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:automaat.html>automaat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-isch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:automatisch.html>automatisch</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:automatisch.html>automatischer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:automatisch.html>automatisch</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">automatischt</b>)

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<dl><dd><i>an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:avenger.html>avenger</a></b> of blood</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>One who <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> vengeance.</li></ol>

***averechts.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a> (42593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">backwards, in the wrong direction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">averecht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">upside down, backwards, wrong</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ave</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechts.html>rechts</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechtser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">averechtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>opposite, backwards, contrary
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkt.html>werkt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>What you're doing now <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the <b>opposite</b> effect of what you're trying to achieve.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:averechts.html>averechts</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>in <a href = vnd.unilang:omgekeerd.html>omgekeerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:richting.html>richting</a>.

***avond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a> (510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âvont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">āvont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēbanþs</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avonden.html>avonden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondje.html>avondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>evening, night</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Just like German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Abend</i>, Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i> includes the <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> until midnight. So while one says in English: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re having a <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> tonight!</i>, one would say in Dutch: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:biertje.html>biertje</a>!</i>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avondeten.html>avondeten</a> (4936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">avonteten</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evening</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meal, food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">supper</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">dinner</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">evening meal</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">avontmael</i>. <dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>Laatste</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:avondmaal.html>Avondmaal</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beroemd.html>beroemd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderij.html>schilderij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Leonardo da Vinci.</i>
<dl><dd><i>The Last Supper <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a famous painting by Leonardo da Vinci.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This word tends to be used only to refer to "regular" dinners <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> at home, not to dinner parties or meals eaten elsewhere, where <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diner.html>diner</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avondeten.html>avondeten</a></i> are much more often used.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avontuur.html>avontuur</a> (3236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aventure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">aventure</i>. The <i><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to influence from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> also affected the pronunciation.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a> (7010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ai</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">aȝȝ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">ey</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwa</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ever, always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">āwo</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">āwa</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ā</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ō</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">age; law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ǣ(w)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ieu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">century</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">century</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂eyu-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">long time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">aois</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">age, period</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Breton_language" class="extiw" title="w:Breton language"><a href = vnd.unilang:breton.html>Breton</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="br">oad</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">age, period</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ævum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eternity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">αἰών</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aiṓn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">aevum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ever, always
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1610–1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="w:The Tempest">The Tempest</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act IV, scene i]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>Do that good miſcheefe, which may make this Iſland / Thine owne for euer, and I thy <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caliban" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Caliban">Caliban</a></i>, / For <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></b> thy foot-licker.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1834</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Taylor_Coleridge" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuel Taylor Coleridge">Samuel <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a> Coleridge</a>, "The Rime of the Ancient Mariner":
<dl><dd>The ship drove fast, loud roared the blast, / And southward <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> fled.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1863</b>, Translation by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catherine_Winkworth" class="extiw" title="w:Catherine Winkworth"><a href = vnd.unilang:catherine.html>Catherine</a> Winkworth</a>:
<dl><dd>Let the <a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>Amen</a> sound from His people again; Gladly for <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> adore Him. (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Praise_to_the_Lord,_the_Almighty" class="extiw" title="w:Praise to the Lord, the Almighty">Praise to the Lord, the Almighty</a>)</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></i> as expression of agreement or affirmation, or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">a ye</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a> yes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or synthesis of both. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">yea</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>yes; yea; a word expressing assent, or an affirmative answer to a question.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> much used in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scottish_English" class="extiw" title="w:Scottish English">Scotland</a>, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_English" class="extiw" title="w:Northern English">north</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language_in_EnglandMidlands" class="extiw" title="w:English language in England">Midlands</a> of England, the northern <a href = vnd.unilang:counties.html>counties</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hiberno_English" class="extiw" title="w:Hiberno English">Ireland</a>, North Wales, as well as in Australia and New Zealand (where it may follow rather than precede a statement). Also notably seen in <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">viva voce</i> voting in legislative <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a>, etc., or in nautical contexts.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yes</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yea</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ayes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An affirmative vote; one who votes in the affirmative.
<dl><dd><i>"To call for the <b>ayes</b> and nays;" "The <b>ayes</b> have it."</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yes</span></li></ul>
</body>

***azen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:azen.html>azen</a> (11646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">asen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:azen.html>azen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to predate [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span>]</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to long [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(after)</span></span>], to desire [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span>]</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:azen.html>azen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:azen.html>azen</a></b>
</p>

***baa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a> (95600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">bäh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mäh</i>; an imitative word.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">onomatopoeia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The characteristic cry or bleating of a sheep.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bleat</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bleating</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">onomatopoeia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">The characteristic cry of a sheep.</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">baaing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">baaed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make the characteristic cry of a sheep.
<ul><li><b>1590-1593</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philip_Sidney" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Philip Sidney">Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Countess_of_Pembroke%27s_Arcadia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Countess of Pembroke | s Arcadia">The Countess of Pembroke's <a href = vnd.unilang:arcadia.html>Arcadia</a></a></i>
<dl><dd>He treble <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></b> for help, but none can get.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1902</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbara_Baynton" class="extiw" title="w:Barbara Baynton">Barbara Baynton</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sally.html>Sally</a> Krimmer; Alan <a href = vnd.unilang:lawson.html>Lawson</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>, <cite>Bush Studies</cite> (Portable Australian Authors: Barbara Baynton), St Lucia |  University of Queensland Press, published 1980, page 44:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The lamb bunted several irresponsive <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> never its dam's udder <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <b>baaing</b> listlessly.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">بَاء</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bāʾ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a> (566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bāne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bana</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*banō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baantje.html>baantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a road, way, path

***baar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baar</a> (25466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bâre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bērō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bērō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to carry, bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Beere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stretcher, <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bahre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a>, stretcher</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baren.html>baren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a>, a stretcher, a litter; a device used to carry someone or something, especially wounded or dead people.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:draagbaar.html>draagbaar</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> on which a dead person <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> displayed before he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> buried.
<ul><li><b>1922</b>, Albert Verwey, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.dbnl.org/tekst/verw008wegv01_01/verw008wegv01_01_0028.htm"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Gerichte <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>Wil</a></a>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>Wanneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stierf.html>stierf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beminden.html>beminden</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:rondom.html>Rondom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baar.html>baar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> d’<a href = vnd.unilang:andre.html>andre</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vraagt.html>vraagt</a>:
<dl><dd>When I died and those that <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> / stand around my <b>dead <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></b> and one asks the other:</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lijkbaar</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lijkbed</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:barre.html>barre</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>, an ingot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of gold or another metal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bart</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bard</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bardaz</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰardʰ-eh₂</i>.
